Quan endeve en le fietge dolor per fregiditat o per humiditat o per grossa ventositat entro que de la sieua normal compleccio sia getat per egressio superflua, e es curat le malaute am aquo que havem dit e no comfereys, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre la sua cervitz, e senhes am tenta tres cauteris segon aquesta forma et aquesta quantitat meteyssa sobre le fietge dejos dels ipocondres, la hon perve le decubit de home. E entromet la extremitat subtil en la aurelha segon la quantitat la qual suffertar puesca le malaute; e aprop sucgeys am aquela per succio fort, e fay aquo motas veguadas, entro que totz les verms sian foro-gitatz.	 Then introduce the needle gently into the ear lobe as much as it can reach without causing harm to the patient; and after that, do what is necessary with strong suction force, removing all the worms thoroughly.
Mays si no obezeysso a tu al ayssiment, lahoras tu opila e claus en le circuit de la canula am cera ayssi cum havem dit; lahoras aministre distillacios las quals han ja esproadas les antics en la curacio dels verms, e atrobaras aquo en le tractat de distillacios.	 If not all the worms are gone at this time, the doctor will pull and close off the circuit of the needle as instructed; then administer the distilled water that has already been used in the previous treatment for worms, holding tightly onto it to be used in the treatise on distillation.
E sia la tua efusio am la qual efundas les olis medicinas en la aurelha am aquest strument del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	 And that is how you finish off with the medical remedies given at this instrument, which is in fact a needle of that sort.
E fay aquela de argent o de eram, dejos streyt, en le qual sia un petit trauc, e am pla desus.	 And take what comes out and put it into another container slightly smaller than the first one.
E donc sia cum empellent a que es en la conquavitat de la canula de continent aqui on sira necessari.	 Then, when you are inserting the needle in the patient's abdomen to drain pus or other fluids, this will be necessary here.
E si vols, pren le ray e envolveys en la extremitat de lu decentment coto, e aprop gieta oli en la concavitat del auziment, o suc de alcuna herba, o aquo que vols de aquestas medicinas en la canula — e aquela es en la aurelha —, e aprop entromet le ray am coto desus e exprem am la tua ma aquel am compressio temprada de lu entro que l’oli sia expellit en la concavitat del auziment e le malaute senta le oli dedintz.	 "If you wish, take the tube and insert it gently into the patient's stomach, or into a cavity of no specific herb, or that which you want from these medicines in an artery - and this is at the wrist - and press against your palm to prevent rapid expulsion from the stomach and the patient feeling pain.
E aquo que sia enfundut en la aurelha sia ja scalfat am foc un petit.	 "And that which is inserted into the artery will also burn on contact with a small flame.
E guarda te que la causa la qual distillaras en l’aurelha no sia trop frega, quar las medicinas de aurelha no suffertan aquo.	 "Remember that if the cause which you are going to inject into the artery is too cold, then these medicines from the artery will not work.
Capitol .vii.	 "Goodbye.
De curacio de opilacio de aurelhas.	 "With care of injecting the artery.
Alcunas veguadas alcus enfantz yeysso dels ventres de lors mayres no-perforatz, e aquo ja accideys en alcus homes, opilacio en le meat de la aurelha per plagua o per carn nada en aquela; e aquesta opilacio alcunas veguadas es fayta en le preon del trau de la aurelha la qual no consiec le vezement, e alcunas veguadas es en las partidas defora.	 "Do not perforate the artery in addition to making a hole through the muscle or flesh; do this for punctures outside of your field only. And puncturing holes should be done on the back side of the artery so that it does not come out, and puncturing holes will have their own separate procedure.
E aquela que accideys en le preon de lu, la qual no comprehen le vezement, es en las majors disposicios de dificil sanacio.	 "And if this happens on the back side of it, which does not comprehend its meaning, is in major difficulties for treatment.
E en aquela en qual consegueys le vezement, cove que tu pauses la aurelha del malaute al solelh e reguarda en aquela.	 In that space where you place a cushion for the patient's thighs, put an additional cushion under their knees, watch over them closely.
E donc si vezes oppulacio apparent, obre aquela am espatum subtil del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	 And if there are times of extreme pain, then apply a more subtle poultice which is the form of it:
Si’ la extremitat de lu en la qual sia petita la latitut, del qual la una partida sia aguda e l’autra no; e le spatum sia de dos latz leon per so que no fassa lizio al aurelha.	 If the extremity of it where small in latitude, such that one part is acute and the other not, then apply a poultice with two layers to prevent injury to the cushion.
E donc si la opilacio es per carn nascuda en la aurelha o en le meat de lu, lahoras te aquela am oncis subtils e incidiys aquela vehement facilitat entro que sia ostada tota la carn.	 Then if application is to be made on naked skin of the thigh or buttocks, apply a poultice with the most delicate and incise the surface so that it penetrates throughout all the flesh.
E si opilacio es en le preon de la aurelha, lahoras pren ray subtil leon e escalfa aquel am foc un pauc, e aprop met aquel en le meat de l’aurelha.	 And if application is to be made on the underside of the thigh, place a very delicate poultice lightly and put it into the meat of the buttocks.
E donc si as scentit oppulacio am aquo que le malaute atroba am facilitat, per gravetat de ausir, esforsa la oppressio de lu am facilitat; e guarda te que no plagues les nervis del aurelha.	 And if the poultice application is so severe that it causes discomfort to the patient due to its severity, try to relieve pressure by ease and keep in mind not to press on the nerves of the thigh.
E aprop pausa en l’aurelha drap de li segon la quantitat del ample del trauc lo qual tu as envolvutz en l’enguent egipciac; e fay aquo per alcus jorns entro que sias segur de la consolidacio de la plagua; o que prenguas qualgua e enfon aquela en ayguaros e pulveriza sobre lu segi trissat e usa de lu; e si vezes la aurelha ja esser apostemada, lahoras cove que tu estraguas la qualgua e permutes aquela am autra qualgua la qual tu envoloparas en cerot que sia fayt am oli rozat, entro que sia le apostema caut cedat; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	 And after applying the poultice to the thigh as described above, wait until you are sure of its consolidation and if necessary add a second poultice which will be placed on top of it in order to soften it, and then pulverize over it with a damp cloth or something similar so that it is moist. If the cushion has already been applied before and has not been removed, apply another poultice as well, being careful not to cause injury while applying them.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras submergeys esponga o drap en aygua frega e pausa sobre la aurelha, e usa del autra curacio la qual restrengeys le flux del sanc, la qual es dita en le tractat de distillacio.	 When the vein flow of blood is impeded, the pain surges up or droops down with fluid that drips and falls on the ear lobe, and another servant uses a certain caution to restrict the flow of blood in order to make it stop.
Capitol .viii.	 The eighth capital
De cura de athezil le qual endeveno a las palpebras.	 To cure the itch that comes from the eyes
Athezil les quals endeveno a las paupebras dels huels alcuna veguada so humitz, alscunas veguadas son secs.	 The itching of the eyelids caused by cold humidity is treated with soft cloths soaked in vinegar or other remedies that are dry.
Donc cove que tu tenguas aquels am tenhalhas o am onci, e inscindas aquels am espatum de las suas razitz, e aprop pausa sobre les locs segi trissat.	 And if you have already opened the space between the ribs and legs, then place your hand over the area to prevent the intestine from coming out.
Mays si dolor am flux de sanc veno, lahoras tu cauteriza aquels am cauteri lanticular subtil.	 When the vein flow of blood is impeded, the pain surges up or droops down with fluid that drips and falls on the ear lobe, and you use a certain caution to restrict the flow of blood in order to make it stop.
E la milhor cauterizacio es aprop las inscizios e tropas veguadas retornam quan reman alcuna causa de sas razitz; e quan so cauterizadas am foc, aquelas razitz son comburidas e no retornan.	 The best caution is to burn the inflamed and irritated areas when they remain without a cause of their inflammation; and once burned, those areas are calmed down and do not return.
Capitol .ix.	 The ninth capital
Cura de grandeyssa que veno a las palpebras dels huels.	 To cure the redness of the eyes
Motas veguadas endeve en las palpebras dels huels alcuna causa la qual es asemblada a grandissa en sa fortalicia e duricia, e per so grandissia es apelada.	 The itching and redness of the eyelids caused by large causes that assemble in their strength and harshness is called for greater care.
E es agreguacio de humiditat grossa en la palpebra dejos e desus.	 Earmuffs
Donc la opperacio en lor es que consideras lahoras si la grandissia es procedent en lu en aquo que apar de la palpebra e es mauguda a tota partida; e la causa de lu es leugiera.	 Therefore, the operation is that when the swelling occurs in this way on the eyelid and covers everything completely, then the cause of it must be liquid or mucus.
Donc fen sobre aquela am fissura per la latitut, e aprop escorga aquela de tota partida am facilitat entro que evasesca, e aprop suspen aquela am onci e abscindeys aquela.	 Then fasten up that tear in the latitude, and let it be as wide as possible so that you can easily remove it, then gently pull off that tear and remove it.
Mays si a tu no es apparelhada la incizio de lu si no pus que penetras la palpebra am inscizio pauc a pauc, lahoras aquo no notz en deguna causa.	 If you are accustomed to puncturing the eyelid at all times but penetrate it only slightly and occasionally, then pain in this case is due to no cause.
E si la figura es gran, lahoras tu l’ajusta am sutura; e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	 If the swelling is great, loosen your sutures and care for it until it heals.
E si es pauca, a tu no sobrevindra mal per aquela quar l’anguent de lu restaura aquela e encarna.	 If it is small then you will not find fault in that vein as long as the rest of its blood supply remains unchanged.
E si la grandissia es declinant a las partidas dedintz de la palpebra deves la superficia dedintz, lahoras evesa la palpebra e suspen la grandissia am onci, otra que tu indigescas de incizio, e prem aquela de tota part, e si la palpebra per inscizio es alonguada, aquo no notz en deguna causa.	 If the swelling is diminishing from all sides of the eyelid and you see it on its surface, then pain in this case is due to no cause.
E aprop la incizio, lava le huel am aygua salada; e cura le loc am aquo que encarna entro que sia sanat.	 Then fasten up the incision, let cool water run over it and care for the area until it heals.
Capitol .x.	 Conclusion.
De la cura axcirnah en la palpebra desus del huel.	 Of cure for this eye-ache in the eyelid of these
Axcirnath es grays le qual es engendrat en las tunicas de la palpebra desus, e majorment endeve als enfantz, agrava les huels de aquels et accideyso a lor catartz le mayti; e no podon reguardar la claror del solelh per aquo quar lagremas se coytan ad aquels.	 Of the cause of this eye-ache in the eyelid of these (people) born with a grey hue, and more prone to children than adults, makes their cheeks reddened and irritates them at sight; so that they may not look directly at those who have it
E per so tu vezes aquels jaser sobre les lors caras tot temps, e sobre les lors caras dormen; e so a las palpebras de lor dejos les sobrecils humidas, las quals ja ha cuberta imflacio, e iminencia de accernac apparent es en l’uelh; e que quant tu premes le loc am les tieus ditz, tu centes accernac entro aquels.	 So that they may sometimes shed tears over the faces of those with it at night and while sleeping; so that their eyelids are wet from the excess of dampness, which has been inflamed by it and is about to burst through its own accord; and when you press on their temples (foreheads), you will find evidence of it.
E alcuna manieyra de opperacio es en aquel que le malaute pausa le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop pausa drap de li e de lu fay calgua, e fay de lu cercle segon la quantitat la qual contena arthernach de tota partida, e aprop pausa aquel sobre aquela e prem am les tieus ditz de tota per que sia agreguat arcernac en le mieg del cercle, e aprop fen en le mieg de aquela humiditat am spatum inscident am fissura per la latitut, e la fissura no sia major que la fissura que es fayta en flaubotomia.	 No matter how many times they try to cover it up with bandage or cloth, the excess of dampness will always escape through a small hole in their forehead, and the small tear that is there will also burst; when you press on their temples (foreheads), you will find evidence of it.
Mays en le preon cove que tu fendas la codena tota entro que pervenguas ad arcernach, quar en las mays desposicios proceseys arcernach per fissura segon la forma de grayseza blanca.	 In the first place you should be sure to have looked through all that comes in contact with it from every direction, and especially for any gray-colored openings, as soon as there is a tear or hole made by this condition.
Donc extratz aquela am draps los quals tu as envolopatz entre les tieus ditz a las partidas deforo e revolv entre la ma dextra e sinistre entro que sia dispargut.	 Then remove that which you have wrapped around between the thighs, leaving it exposed and roll it up between your right hand and left hand until it is smooth.
E guarda te que no ajustes en la fissura per so que am le spatum no pervenguas al huel e ladescas aquel.	 Then cover it to prevent any damage from occurring on the scrotal skin, which could potentially cause injury or harm.
Mays si no apar a tu arternach en le comensament de la fissura, mays que tu ajustes en la fissura un petit am fecilitat entro que procesisca arternach; e aprop extratz aquela ayssi quo havem dit; e aprop submargeys draps de li en aygua e vi agre e pausa les sobre le loc e estrenh aquels am polvils.	 If not already applied, put it on the beginning of the tear to prevent any contact with the scrotal skin during this time, and then remove it afterwards; and proceed as follows:
E so alcus que trissan sal e pausan aquel en la conquavitat de la fissura per so que aquo que es remas de aquela humiditat.	 And do so that you apply some salt in the cavity of the tear to prevent any excess moisture from remaining there.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	 Then take care of it until it is healed.
Mays si accideys en le loc apostema caut, lahoras cura aquel am emplastres cedatils entro que sia sanat.	 If the cut happens to be deep, then apply pressure to help prevent excessive blood loss and take care of it until it is healed.
Capitol .xi.	 11th chapter
De manieyras de tactimi del huel.	 Various types of treatment for the foot.
Quan en las palpebras dels huels so natz pels ajustatz dejos les pels naturals e so antiquatz, lahoras aquels noso al huel e fan endevenir manieras de malautias ayssi cum lacrimas assiduas e mollificacio de palpebras e tela entro que aquo sia causa de destruccio del huel que s’apela tactinir del huel, e cura se en quatre manieyras: o per cauteri am foc; o am medicina acuta segon que denant es dit en le capitol de cauteri; o es fayt atactini per inscizio e sutura; o per cannas segon que yeu diyre.	 When examining the hands of the patient, you must check for natural burns and artificial wounds, then apply ointments containing astringents to heal them and prevent further damage from occurring, or else it could lead to destruction of the hand which is called "hand necrosis", and there are four types of treatment: cautery with fire; treatment by an acute medicine as mentioned in the chapter on cautery; use of stitches for wounds; or use of bandages.
E donc cove que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se; aprop converteys la palpebra del uelh am la tua ma sinistra, e si es convertida, bo es; e sino, entromet agulha en aquela en la qual sia fiel de la partida pus dejos de la palpebra, e fay penetrar la agulha am fiel desus, e aquo sia — prop del marge de la palpebra en le qual naysso les pels — prop dels pels, e tira le fiel a las partidas desus am la palpebra, e converteys aquela am le ray.	 "You should remove the cap from the patient's head and tie his left hand to your own left hand.
E aprop fen en la partida dedintz de la palpebra dejos les pels ajustatz am spatum inscidentz del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal mendre; e aprop extratz le fiel e pausa dejos la palpebra polvilhs petitz de coto o de drap, e aprop senha sobre la palpebra am tenta, e sia ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirt.	 "Secure the eyelid in a fold and attach it to the lower lid, then gently remove the bandage or cloth from the eye, and place your hand over the eye.
Mays empero cove que sia la figura segon la quantitat de helevacio de la palpebra, quar aquo ja es diversificat en les homes, quar de aquels es le quals indigeys que sia inscidit de la palpebra gran quantitat segon la quantitat per la qual la palpebra es mollificada.	 "Please note that this step varies based on the amount of swelling around the eyelid, as it can vary in different individuals depending on how much swelling is present.
E aprop fen am le spatum sobre las doas linhas las quals has senhadas, e comensa del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal menor.	 "Take one hand and place it above the two lines you have just drawn, then bring your other hand from the lower lid to the upper.
E si’ la tua fissura prop dels pels naturals ayssi cum es la grossetut del rey.	 "If natural tears flow as strongly as those in this example, do not worry.
E aprop met le onci en un dels dos angles de la codena, e aprop excoria aquela tota, e aprop ajusta am la scitura las doas labias am gula o fiel de lana subtil, e abstergeys le sanc, e fay adherir aquo que superflueys dels fiels sobre dos sobrecils am alcunas causas enviscans, si voles far aquo, e sino, non cures.	 "Place the spoon in one of two corners of a piece of bread and spread it across, then arrange both ends into a loop on top of your thumb or index finger; if you wish to do so, otherwise do not.
E aprop leyssa la sutura dels fiels entro a tres dias o quatre, e aprop cura aquo.	 The wound of the field will be healed within three days or four
E si vols, layssa la plagua ses sutura, e cura aquela am aquo que exsicca e constrenh, quar la palpebra es alevada deves la sigillacio de la plagua e la agreguacio de lu; mays sutura es milor E donc aysso diysso les antics de taxanir.	 If you wish to heal the wound of the field quickly and efficiently, then remove all the moisture from it and stretch out its area as much as possible; may this healing be better than previous ones.
Mays empero en lu sia sollicitut sobre le malaute, e es de bona operacio, e no es en lu temor.	 And maybe in that way the patient will get well quickly and efficiently, without any fear.
E es autra manieyra en taxmir, e es que senhes sobre la palpebra figura ayssi cum fuelha de mirt, e aprop eleva la palpebra am tres uncis segreguatz e congreguatz segon aquesta forma:	 This other remedy in question is to apply it directly on the patient's eye as soon as possible, and after applying this way, elevate the patient's hand with three fingers spread out;
Mays si no es possible aquo, tener les uncis, e aquo no es engualhat, lahoras pren una agula en la qual haia fil e met aquela en le mieg de la figura, e entromet le autre fiel prop le lacrimal major, e·l fiel segon prop le lacrimal mendre, e ajusta entre les tieus ditz les fiels am equalitat, e aprop am aquels eleva la tua ma am elevacio engual, eleva tota la codena sobre la qual es senhat ayssi cum havem recomtat.	 If it is not possible to do this way then take a needle with which you can pierce the eye and put it on that spot; enter another finger near the upper tear duct, one further near the lower one, and adjust between those fingers so that they are equally distant from each other, and after applying this elevation, raise your hand high in elevation, elevating all the way up to where is recommended as such.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	 Then place both lips of the wound together and heal it into shape.
Mays si accideys apostema deves la tua inscizio o la tua fissura, seda aquel apostema am cerot e a lu semblantz, e am enguentz.	 If you cut your finger or hand off entirely, place that part of the body near and bind it to itself with twine; this is how you heal it.
E alcunas veguadas endeve a la palpebra que·ls sieus pels sian convertitz, adonc cove que tu uses en aquela de aquo que havem dit de inscizio; mays sutura en quascus es mays artificial.	 "The eye is being squeezed between the eyelids," meaning that someone has placed pressure on both eyelids to prevent blinking or closing of the eyes.
Ataxinir am cannas es segon aquesta forma:	 To perform this task, you will need a cannula and some anesthetic agent (or anaesthetic).
e es que tu convertas la palpebra e scindas la figura qu’es dedintz segon que he recontat; e aprop per art fay doas cannas o doas astelas subtils de las quals longitut sia segon la longitut de la palpebra e la latitut de lor sia mendra de la latitut del spatum.	 This means that you should stretch the eyelid and divide it into two parts as described in step 2, ensuring they are aligned in length (from top to bottom) and angle relative to your finger.
E tu ja has inscidit en las extremitatz de quascunas partidas, la on tenes les fils.	 You have injected into the extremities of both parts where you hold them.
Aprop agregua quascuna am subtilitat subre aquo que superflueys de la palpebra del huel, e constres las cannas de quascunas partidas am fort strictura, e layssa aquela per alcus jorns, quar la codena per la strictura morira e sira denegada e se poyrira entro que per si meteyssa cayra.	 Tighten the cannula of each part very gently so that it does not interfere with vision or cause any discomfort for extended periods.
Mays si es tardat, lahoras trenca la am las toroyras, e aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanat.	 If it's late and the wound is infected, then take care of the patient and treat the wound as necessary.
Donc cum es solidada, la palpebra es elevada e les pels no pungo.	 Once the procedure has been completed successfully (i.e., you have stretched and divided the eyelid into two equal parts), there will be no squeezing or pulling sensation felt by the patient.
E aquesta es la forma de doas cannas las quals faras segon aquesta forma:	 This is how to perform this task using both cannulas
e haia la quantitat de la longitut e de la latitut ni mays ni mens.	 There should be no minimum or maximum length and angle measurements for either part of the eyelid.
Capitol .xii.	 When joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, and pain occurs in the feet, it is customarily called gout by doctors.
De elevacio de pels pungentz en le huel am agula quan le pel es dur.	 The physician makes a small incision into the flesh to relieve the pain.
Quan son pels no-naturals, durs e aspres e pungentz les huels, lahoras la operacio en lu es que tu prenguas agula subtil e pauses en aquela fiel de ceda subtil e leon, e aprop que tu ajustes las extremitatz de lu e nozes quascu en manieyra mot subtil.	 If the pain is not natural and harsh, but occurs in the joints themselves, then the procedure is to make a small incision into the flesh there; hold it with a sharp pointed instrument close enough so that you adjust both of its extremities gently without losing sight of the tiny hole.
E sia la longitut dels fiels de quantitat de una palma.	 The length of the incision should be about equal to the size of one palm.
E aprop tu compon2 autre fiel subtil dejos lu en breu, e nuza las extremitatz de aquel si tu·t vols.	 Then you put another small needle next to it and fix its position if you wish.
E aprop pause le malaute le sieu cap en le tieu se, e sia prop del solelh per que la tua obra sia declarada, quar es operacio subtil e menuda.	 Then hold the patient's head gently in place and secure it to prevent its movement during the subtle procedure.
E aprop intromet la agulha en la razit del pel ajustat la qual ha necessitat de engen, e fay aquela penetrar en la palpebra festinantment entro que extraguas aquela desus le pel natural.	 Then insert the needle into the flesh with its point adjusted to pierce through as needed; make sure it penetrates just beneath the natural skin layer so that you can extract any necessary tissue.
E aprop tire le pel entro desus e intromet aquel en alixati, e sian les pels un o dos o tres e no mays.	 Then take away the flesh between them and insert it into place; sew up one or two or three stitches to close the incision.
E aprop tira la tua ma am aquel entro que·l pel sia fora-gitat am alixolati en la palpebra am le pel natural.	 Then take away your hand from that part of the flesh and gently pull it out through the small hole in the skin, making sure not to pull it out too hard as you do this.
Mays si es atirat alixalati e non es gitat le pel, atiraras alixati a las partidas dejos am le fiel le qual tu has compost am aquela, entro qu’en sia gitat alixalati del trau sobira.	 When the joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, and pain occurs in the feet, it is customarily called gout by doctors.
E vegas aquela am la visio del huel, quar lahoras tu gitaras alixati e lo fiel, e grotan quascu e clautz le huel, e laysse le claus per dos dias o tres, entro que·l pel adheresca al sieu loc e nasque sobre aquel bona carn.	 The physician will examine the affected area closely, making sure to feel around it and gently press on any tender spots, and lay a cloth over it for two or three days until the pain subsides from that place and arises no more at another location.
E si es mays breu le pel, lahoras tu ajusta un pel lonc dels pels naturals, e es elevat am aquel, o que·l leysses entro que sia alonguat aprop alcu spazi, e lehoras tu eleva aquel.	 If the joint pain is severe and pressing on the skin, the physician will use a gentle touch to apply an ointment of natural substances onto it, or if that doesn't alleviate the problem then they should gently lift up the affected part and hold it there until the pain subsides from that location only.
Capitol .xiii.	 Chapter 13.
De la cura de ehacratir la qual ve en la palpebra desus.	 Of curing an inflammation in the eyelid.
Quan ve en le huel ehacratir, e es contraccio de la palpebra quan es contrayta en sus, o a dextra o a sinistra partida, per mala consolidacio de plagua o de seccio o de cauteri, e es apelada leporina, e aquesta ahercrati o es natural o accidental, e es fayta per consolidacio de plagua o de seccios o de cauteri, o per semblantz a lor malcuratz. Mays si la dent es trauquada o corrosa, lahoras cove que tu comples de drap aquel trauc e estrenguas aquel am la extremitat de ray subtil per so que no sia trinquada en la hora de la tua constriccio sobre aquela am tenalas. E guarda te que no fassas aquo que fan alscus ignorantz barbiers en lor fistinacio e audacia sobre la eradicacio de lor, ses que no aministran aquo que nos havem recomtat; quar motas veguadas fan venir sobre les homes malautias grans las quals son pus dificils que sian trinquadas, e las razitz de lor remaugudas totas, o alcunas de aquelas, o que extrayguas aquela am alcus osses de la mandigula ayssi cum motas veguadas havem testificat. E aprop la eradicacio de lu sia lavada la boca am vi caut o vi agre am sal.	 "Wash away the discharge from their mouth gently or wash it off quickly.
E si endeve fluxs de sanc per aysso, ayssi cum motas veguadas endeve, lahoras trissa alcuna quantitat de zegi e aspergeys sobre la plagua, e si no confereys aquel zegi, cauteriza.	 "If you encounter difficulties in cutting the discharge, first cleanse it gently or quickly wash it off.
La forma de las forceps e tenalas subtils am las quals es mauguda la dent al comensament sia de longua extramitat, de breu manubre e gros, per so que no sian doblatz quan am aquels deves obrar. E sian faytas de ferr de India descentment faytas de dreytas extramitatz, e en las extramitatz de aquelas sian dentz de las quals las unas intron en las autras e estrenhan per constriccio descent fort, e alscunas veguadas las extramitatz de aquelas sian la forma del bec d’un auzel le qual ha nom ciconia, so es guanta, e son de fort constriccio. de la triangulada extremitat torta o curta, la qual sia alcuna grossesa, e no sia enbegut per so que no sia trinquat.	 The tip should be triangular in length or short with an appropriate size that is not too small to tear.

Capitol .xxxii.	 Chapter XXXII
De la cura de las dentz eminentz sobre las autras.	 The care of teeth is more important than the other organs.
Quan las dentz so eminentz no segon lor cors natural per aquelas la forma es laga, e majorment quan endeve a las femnas, e majorment a las piuselas venerablas; donc cove que tu consideras: si dent es nada aprop autra dent, e no es possibla sarradura ni linament de lu, lahoras radica aquela; mays que no sia annexa am autra dent, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am aquest instrument del qual aquesta es la forma; e es semblant a morr de porc, e sia feyt de ferr de India de extramitat mot aguda.	 When the teeth are prominent and do not fit into their natural place, and especially when they cause pain to women or girls, then the doctor will remove them. However if another tooth is necessary for biting, and it cannot be removed without causing damage, the doctor will consider that tooth separately with this instrument which is used as such; and it's similar to cutting off a pig's tail, except that it must be done very carefully from India to prevent injury
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscideyses aquela en trops dias per la duricia de la dent, e que no sia comauguda autra de las dentz.	 When a toothache occurs in days of hardship, it is customary that one makes an incision with this to remove the tooth, and not to cause any other harm to the teeth
E si es dent eminent expausat a limadura, lahoras lima aquel am lima de ferr de India del qual aquesta es la forma:	 If it is necessary to extract a wisdom tooth, the doctor shall perform this incision in that manner from which follows.
E sia tot de ferr de India e·l margua eysament; e sia de motz menutz puntz ayssi cum lima am la qual son faytas agulhas, am la qual la dent sia limada pauc a pauc en motz dias am fecilitat, per so que no sia autra dent comauguda e caga.	 To extract the tooth with India ink; first make an incision, and then use a pointed instrument to remove it gently in days of weakness, for fear that another tooth does not come out or cause harm.
E aprop lineys aquela en la fi, e ratz aquela am alscus razoris.	 After the completion of this procedure, you will take care of any other injuries as well.
E si es dent del qual una partida es trinquada e lideys la lengua, lahoras cove que tu limescas aquel entro que l’aspretat de aquela fraccio sia ostada e engualhada, e sia aplenada per so que la lengua no ledesca ni la paraula no corrumpa. Capitol .xxxiii.	 Chapter XXXIII.
De restauracio de dentz maugudas am fiel de aur o de argent.	 Restoration of teeth should be done with gold or silver.
Quan accideys a las dentz devant concussio e remossio per percussio o per cazament, e le malaute no pot strenher sobre aquo que manga, e tu has curat aquel am medicinas stipticas, e no ha valgut la tua curacio, lahoras per so que no cagan es engen en aquelas que sian strengudas am fiel de aur e no de argent, quar argent se fa vert e aprop se poyreys aprop alscus dias, mays aur nul temps no es mudat. E sia le fiel en tal subtilitat e grocesa segon la quantitat que puesca entrar entre las dentz; e la forma de la reccio es que prenguas le fiel e pren lo doble de lu entre doas dentz sanas, e aprop que cresques am doas tortuositatz del fiel entre doas maugudas, o si’ una o motas, entro que pervengua la tela a la dent sana del autra partida. E sia la tua striccio am la qual strenhas le fiel deves las razitz de las dentz que no evasesca.	 "The shape of the hole should correspond exactly to that which you stretch out the faithful, or else it will miss.
E aprop inscindeys las extramitatz del fiel superfluens am las forceps o tosoyras, e agregua aquelas en quascun loc am gesti, e converteys aquelas e las occulta entre la dent sana e la dent mauguda, per so que no fassa lesio a la lengua. E aprop leyssa aquela ayssi streyta cum roman.	 "And then stretch it out with Roman style.
Mays si es desliada o rumpuda, strenh aquela o aquelas am autra fiel en tal manieyra en tot son temps.	 "If you are in doubt or if the faithful is torn, stretch that one and any others at your other hand simultaneously.
E aquesta es la forma de las dentz e la figura de la rectacio de doas dentz sanas e de doas maugudas, ayssi cum vezes aquestas liadas:	 "This is the form of teeth and shape of alignment between two healthy teeth and two damaged ones. Thus:
E quan se fa que retorno una dent o doas aprop le cazement de quascuna en lors locs, e sian recrescutz ayssi cum havem recomtat, e que remauguan.	 "When you return one tooth or two of them to the cutting area in that location, they should be shaped as advised and cut off.
E no fa aquo sino bo artifexs e savi.	 And it doesn't hurt at all

Capitol .xxxiv.	 Chapter forty-four
De inscizio del liament le qual ve en la lengua e prohibeys loquela.	 This is a slit in the membrane of the tongue that prevents speaking.

Capitol .xxxvi.	 When pain arises in joints caused by cold humors infiltrating every part of the body, as well as when pains occur on feet

Capitol .xxxvii.	 When joints are affected by cold humors that penetrate each part of the body, causing pain in the feet, it's customary for doctors to call this gout.
De inscizio de huvela quan es apostemada.	 The incision has been made
Quan catarr deysen a la huvula, e es apostemada e es longa, lahoras ela es nompnada perpendicular; e si es en la partida dejos grossa e redonda, e lahoras ela es apelada buba.	 When the abscess is on the ulcer and it's long, doctors call it a perpendicular abscess; if it's in the great or round part of the body, they call it a bubonic abscess.
Mays quan es curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio, e no comfereys la tua curacio, e eyssament ja vezes que apostema caut ja es ostat de lu e es subtil, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquela que es agreguadas redonda; e si es ad aquela longitut, e es sanguina, de fusca color o de negre, e no es a lu centiment, lahoras cove que tu temtes la inscizio de lu, quar en aquela es temor sobre le malaute.	 When curing occurs in this division and does not affect your cure, and especially if you have already made a puncture with a sharp needle, doctors say that the abscess is cured by puncturing it gently; however, if it's long enough to be bloody or black and doesn't go out through the center of the body, doctors suggest making an incision into it to prevent its appearance.
E quan tu vezes aquela segon la manieyra que yeu he dita de la sua blancor e longuesa, que tu fassas sezer le malaute e premas la lengua de lu am instrument del qual procesic la sua forma e aprop fica le onci en la nuva, e tira aquela en jos e inscideys aquela am un de dos instrumentz les quals e ditz en la inscizio de dos mellas.	 When you see that the ulcer has become white and long enough to reach through it, then make an incision into its center by placing a sharp instrument in your hand; remove the tongue from it gently and insert this same instrument into the new incision made on the other side of the body, and take it out of there and make another incision with one or two instruments depending on which you want to use for making an opening.
E cove que no inscidas aquela sino aquo que es ajustat sobre le terme natural ses addicio, quar si tu inscides de lu mays, lediyras le sieu parlar. De castracio.	 Castration
Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias. E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.	 And therefore it is said that castration must be performed in two ways: either by pulling out or making an incision.
Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan. Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra. De curacio de las plaguas.	 "With regard to the sores.

Del instrument, sec se la forma de lu:	 From the instrument itself

Mays si claudicacio e nodacio son recentz, lahoras cove que sian enbrocatz am aygua tebeza en la qual so coytas erbas mollificantz, ayssi cum son fuelas de altea e razitz de lu, e mellilot, e semblantz ad aquels; e sia fayt a lu emplastre am emplastre mollificatio ayssi cum dyallaquilon ben fayt; o que sia preza mucillage de razit de altea e sia contucida am gray de gualina o am oli de cirami, e sia emplastrat am aquel; o que sian prezes figuas grassas e sian trissadas am fems de colom, e semblantz ad aquels de las medicinas que son nompnadas amermans consolidacio.	 "If recent claudication and numbness occur along with the swelling of certain parts of the body, such as swelling in the feet or legs, it means that the leeches should be applied to the affected areas to alleviate inflammation.
E alcunas vetz es dissolvuda am assidua fricacio leugiera que sia am las mas humidas, e sia administrat movement del membre a tota partida en totas horas.	 When some veins are dissolved by cold humidity they cause leg pain that occurs during the day and lasts for hours.
Mays si tortuositat ja es anada denant e es fayta fort e convertida es en peyra e provocada es necessitat a curacio de lu am ferr, lahoras cove que sia le pus desus cecsat e la continuacio del os sia dissolvut, e sia inscidit aquo que superflueys de nodacio de aquel meteys am le os am inscissoris subtils, e sia aministrada facilitat en aquel am sollicitut e studi.	 The tortuous veins become rigid and twisted as a result of cold humidity; they must be treated with care to prevent further complications, such as the dissolution or bursting of the veins themselves, which may lead to the loss of small capillaries due to the delicate nature of their rupture, and it should be done in a manner that avoids causing harm to nearby tissues while still achieving its goal.
Capitol .xxiii.	 Chapter 33
De sermo en dislocacio.	 On Dislocation
Dislocacio es eyssiment de alcuna de las juncturas del sieu loc, per que es prohibida de movement, e es orrezada la figura del membre, e fa venir sobre le malaute dolors e lesios grans.	 A dislocation is the act of forcibly separating a joint from its place, which prevents movement and results in severe injuries to the member.
Donc quan accideys ad alcu dislocacio, lahoras cove tantost perforsar que sia reduzit, e no tarde aquela reduzir, quar si es tardada, le loc es apostemat e fort leu am aquo es fayta dificil la reduccio de dislocaccio.	 When an accident occurs with a dislocation, doctors must act quickly to reduce it, and not let any delay pass by in which case the joint is separated from its place, causing severe damage and making reduction of dislocation difficult.
E per aysso no cove que sia maugut ni stendut en la hora de la apostemacio, quar motas veguadas fa venir spasme e dolors ledentz.	 And thus it cannot be that they should be held back or restrained during the time of the reduction procedure, as spasms and pain may come to light.
Mays quan aquo accideys, lahoras cove que tu te coytes a la flaubotomia del malaute, e aprop sia layssat entro que repause le apostema; e aprop le membre sia embrocat am aygua cauda e oli, e aprop sia reduzit am facilitat.	 When that happens, doctors should proceed to the cautery of the patient's foot and place their hand over it to prevent the intestine from coming out, then return it back into its cavity; apply wet water and oil to the member and reduce in a manner that is easy.
E tot membre sia curat am aquo del qual la rememoracio vindra en son loc.	 The first member being treated here will bring memory back into its location.
E yeu ja e ordenatz les capitols de dislocacio segon que es precedit en fractura; de la partida del cos pus sobirana entro a la partida pus dejos.	 After the previous dislocation of the limb, begin from the point where the fracture occurred towards the opposite side.
Capitol .xxiiii.	 The twenty-fourth chapter.
De curacio de dislocacio de la mandibula dejos.	 Treatment for dislocation of the jaw is as follows...
So dislocadas las doas mandibulas si no tart; e la dislocacio de amdos es fayta segon una de dos manieyras: que o son remaugudas de lurs locs per pauca remocio, e so mollificadas un petit; o so dislocadas per entiera dislocacio e complida, entro que sian mollificadas a la partida de la junctura entro que corro saliva del malaute e que no puesca tenir aquela ni puesca claure la sua boca, e la lengua de lu sia envolopada en sa paraula.	 If the two jaws cannot be reduced by little force (the first method), they are dislocated and held open by a third party, with their mouths closed to prevent saliva from escaping; or if this is not possible, then perform a complete dislocation into which saliva must run out and the patient's tongue is covered over his mouth.
Mays quan la dislocacio de lu es pauca, lahoras en las majors disposicios retorna per si an pauca causa.	 When the dislocation is slight, the pains return in a great many ways.
Mays si la dislocacio es entiera e complida, lahoras cove que sia administrada reduccio de lu leugierament, e no sia tardada de tot.	 If the dislocation is complete and painful, then treatment for it should immediately be given, and not delayed at all.
E es que·l ministre tengua le cap del malaute, e entrometa lo metge le dit pous de la una sieua ma en la razit de la dislocacio de la mandibula dedintz la boca de lu, si la dislocacio es de la una part; o que entrometa les sieus dos pouzes ensemps, si la dislocacio es de doas partz, e les autres ditz de las mas de lu sian defora am les quals enguale; e comanda al malaute que cesse las suas mandibulas e absolva aquelas anar de quascuna partida; e le metge engualhe la mandibula e enpellisca la mandibula entro que retorne al sieu loc.	 The minister shall hold the patient's head, and have his mouth open for the treatment of dislocation of one jaw only (if partial) or both jaws simultaneously if there are two dislocations; and in either case have another servant remove those that are further away from where they should go, so as to align them properly. And command the patient to close their jaws and allow them to fall back into place; then the surgeon shall open the mouth again and pull it back into position.
E si dificil es la reducio de lu, e majorment si amdos las mandibulas so essemps dislocadas, lahoras aministra evoporacio am aygua cauda e oli, entro que sia fayta leugiera la reduccio de amdos e no tardes la reduccio de amdos de tot, ayssi quo havem dit.	 When joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, and pain occurs in the feet, it is customary to call gout by doctors.
E donc cum retornam e so engualadas, e es clausa la boca del malaute e no es mollificada, lahoras pausa sobre aquelas polvils de drap am cerot, e sia fayt de cera e oli rozat; e aprop sia liat am facilitat am liamens mols.	 Then return the intestine or hernia to its cavity, and place your hand over the area to prevent the intestine from coming out.
E sia le dormir del malaute sobre le sieu dos, e·l cap de lu sia stant entre dos aurelhes, per so que no maugue aquel a la partida dreyta ni a la sinistra; e no li fassas per forsa masteguar alcuna causa; habans la sieua vianda sia forbicio leon, entro que quan las dolors sian remaugudas e las mandibulas so nozadas, lahoras maugue aquo que vol.	 Then place the patient's head between two pillows to prevent it from rolling to either side; and do not let any other cause a disturbance of its position; have established their base as requested, when the pains subside and the mouth is closed, you may proceed
E aquo sia aministrat am facilita, e no trebalhe sobre la apercio de la boca deves la comestio e beure e ocitatio, entro que la mandibula sia nozada e sanada.	 Then administer the medication that is to be given through this opening of the mouth; and drink water as requested when the mouth is opened; having closed it after having given or taken the medicine, and having made sure the mouth has been rinsed
E si es dificil la reduccio de duas mandibulas quan so dislocadas en alcuna hora e no so convertidas als lors locs, lahoras motas veguadas accideysso febres e soda assidua, e fort leu es alerguat le ventre del malaute, e fort leu e vomeys colera pura.	 If it is difficult to reduce both mouths at the same time and they are not converted into the correct positions during the day or night; then after a bath of vinegar and salt water, and having drunk pure cold water, do you get heartburn from the patient's belly, and suffer severe and frequent attacks of colic.
E quan tu vezes aquo, lahoras sapias que es perdicio; e motas veguadas mor aquel al qual accideys aquo en x dias.	 When you do this, the pains disappear; and sometimes it lasts until the person who gets that affliction meets with something like it in a certain number of days
Capitol .xxv.	 Chapter 25
De reduccio de la dislocacio de la furcula e de la extremitat del muscle.	 Correction of dislocation of the shoulder and arm extremity
Furcula no es dislocada del latz dedintz per la sua continuacio am le pietz; e alcunas veguadas es dislocada a la partida defora, e aquo es declarat al sentiment.	 The furcula is not dislocated by the continued pressure on its chest; and some patients are dislocated at the outset of treatment, as indicated here.
E la restauracio de lu es que·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu dos e extenda les sieus brasses.	 The restoration procedure is that the patient lies flat on their back and extends their limbs.
E aprop coarta le loc am la tua palma am fort coartacio, quar ela retornara.	 With a firm grasp at its base, where it returns to place itself
E aprop pausa sobre aquela emplastre e pulvils e strenh aquela.	 Place your hand gently on the pad and pulp of that [area], and strain lightly over there.
Mays la extremitat de aquel que siec le coyde e·s continuat am aquel, no es dislocada en alcun dia; lahoras cove que sia reduzida e engualhada segon que havem dit e segon que es a tu aparelhat. E am aquesta meteyssa curacio es reduzida la extremita del muscle quan es separada del sieu loc.	 The procedure of reduction is reduced when the extremity is separated from its place.
Capitol .xxvi.	 Chapter 26
De la reduccio de la dislocacio del muscle.	 Correction of dislocation of the limb.
Sapias que·l muscle no es dislocat sino segon tres manieras, de las quals es la una que sia dislocat a la partida del titillic a la partida dejos.	 The first sentence translates to "The muscle is not dislocated, but only in three ways, one of which it is dislocated at the start of the thigh and another at the end of the thighs.
E la segonda es que sia dislocat a la partida desus del muscle, e aquo es fayt tart; e no es dislocat a las partidas detras per la spalla; e no es dislocat a las partidas denant per les nervis.	 The second sentence translates to "And the second way is that it is dislocated at the start of its muscle, and this is done with caution; and it is not dislocated from behind on the back; and it is not dislocated in front by the nerves.
E majorment es dislocat e defora eyssit a las partidas dejos deves le titillic, e majorment en aquels dels quals las carns son paucas, leugierament es dislocat; mays en aquels en les quals so motas carns, es eyssit fora am dificultat.	 "Furthermore, if dislocated in the place where the bones are scarce, it is done with great care; meanwhile, if in those in which the movements of the limbs are less, it is done with difficulty; and also on those that have fewer movements, it is done outside with greater difficulty.
E fort leu accideys ad alcus homes percussio o cazement, e le muscle de lu es apostemat de apostema caut, e es cujat per aquo que ja sia dislocat.	 "If the blow strikes forcefully on these bones and the muscle is dislocated with caution, then it is done in such a way that it has already been dislocated.
Adonc cove que tu sproes aquo entro que estias sobre-sertetut de lu, e lahoras procesiscas en la curacio de lu.	 "Furthermore, once you are above the level of his chest, the physician will proceed to examine him with great care.
E es conoguda la dislocacio de lu quan es a las partidas dejos deves le titillic; per so que distingescas entre le muscle dislocat e·l muscle sa, quar tu atrobas entre aquels diversitat manifesta; e atrobas en le cap del muscle concavitat e dejos le titillic deves le tocament del cap del muscle ayssi quo un huou, e al malaute no pot redusir la sua ma a la sieua aurelha, ni maure aquela per totz movementz.	 "You can distinguish between the dislocated and the normal muscle by noting whether there is concavity at its end or if it is straight; you also look for the concavity of the thigh bone and note how much motion in that direction it has, so that one hand cannot reduce to the head of the muscle without moving all over.
Si es dislocat deves le pietz o ensus, e tu lahoras atrobas manifest tocament, e no es amaguat.	 When joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, it causes pain in the feet as well, and it is customarily called gout by doctors.
E de aquesta dislocacio es fayta leugiera reduccio quan es fresca e le malaute es enfant.	 If this dislocation occurs when fresh and the patient is warm, do reduce its size quickly, otherwise not to be concerned.
E la reduccio de lu es que·l ministre eleva la ma de lu a las partidas desus; e aprop pause les tieus pouses dejos le titillic de lu, e eleva la junctura am fortaleza en sus al sieu loc, e·l ministre eleva la ma de lu, e extenda aquela en sus; e aprop pausa aquela dejos quar ela retorna leugierament.	 The reduction of it should be made while lifting the patient's hand to their chest, and placing a cushion under them as well, so that no parts are harmed by the motion.
Mays si per aquo que havem dit no retorna, e so del comensament que accidic la dislocacio, motz dias, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia banhat en aygua cauda e sia aministrada enbrocacio que mollifique e liniesca ayssi cum si so coytz razitz de altea, e fenugrec, e melillot en aygua, e sia administrada.	 If you have previously said not to return it or if the procedure is just starting, then days later, doctors should ensure that the patient's feet are elevated and moist with a compress, which will help soothe any discomfort caused by swelling, friction, and chills from the injury itself as well as treatment.
E aprop le malaute sia ressupinat sobre le sieu dos e sia pausat dejos le titillic de lu espera de lana que sia engual entre levitat e strictura, e aprop le metge pause le sieu talo sobre la spera, e eleva le cap del muscle am vertut, e atire la ma del malaute per que no sia mauguda a las partidas dejos, e autre ministre tengua le cap del malaute, que no sia maugut a las partidas dejos, quar aquela tantost retorna al sieu loc.	 And hold the patient's head up with support so that it does not fall back down during lifting and straining, and place your hand over their mouth to prevent choking or gagging as well, while another minister holds the head of the muscle at its top, and have a cushion placed under the patient's arm to keep them from being hurt by supporting their upper body.
E si voles, reduzeys aquel segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu fassas esser prezent un home le qual sia pus lonc que·l malaute, e estia de la part de aquel latz, e entrometa le sieu muscle dejos le titillic del malaute e eleve le titillic de lu a las partidas desus entro que·l malaute sia suspendut en ayre, e autre ministre tire la ma del malaute de las partidas dejos del sieu ventre.	 "If you want to, then reduce that second man's member in the same way: and it is customary for you to have a servant present who is large enough to be able to reach into the patient's side, from which he will remove the testicles of the patient and lift them up towards your shoulder. And another servant should take hold of the patient's scrotum and gently pull him out through his belly.
Mays si le malaute es leugier, lahoras cove que am lu que autre causa sia suspenduda, per so que grave aquel, quar la dislocacio retorna tantost.	 "If a hernia is likely to occur, then the doctor orders that another servant should be suspended so that it cannot move around.
E es reduzit eysament segon autra manieyra: e es que sia ficat en terra un fust lonc le cap del qual sia redon de figura, ayssi cum pilo de mortier, que no sia gros ni subtil, e aprop sia pausat dejos le malaute; pus que so pausatz sobre·l cap del fust draps leons, e·l malaute sia stant segon la longitut del fust, e aprop sia extenduda la ma de lu a las partidas dejos del autra part; e sia extendut le cos de lu del autre part am fortaleza, quar la junctura retorna al sieu loc am velocitat.	 "You then proceed with another servant: and that you have placed on the top of his head someone whose body is broad but not too thick or soft, so that they can be lifted up by the patient's hands and held firmly while he moves around; and place your hand over the other part to prevent it from leaving. And extend the body of him with the strength required for the joint movement, as the hernia returns back to its place in a hurry.
E si es dificil reduccio de lu per totas las causas que havem ditas, lahoras usa de aquesta cura: e es que tu prenguas un fust la quantitat del qual sia en le lonc de dos brasses, e latitut de aquel sia de quatre ditz, e la grossetut de lu sia aleujat en le preon del tittilic segon aquesta forma:	 "If the reduction is difficult due to all the causes mentioned before, then the doctor uses this cure. And it is customary for you to take a cushion that has the length of two fists and width of four fingers, and its thickness should be as little as possible.
E aprop sobre le cap redon sian liatz drap leons per so que·l fust no ledesca le malaute.	 The physician approaches the patient's head to prevent the fall of the hernia into their face.
E aprop sia pausat dejos le titillic del malaute, e sia extenduda la ma o le bras sobre·l fust entro a las partidas dejos, e sia liat le fust sobre le adjutori e le bras e la extremitat de la ma.	 The physician places the patient's thighs and extends his hand or arm above the face to prevent the hernia from falling into their face.
Aprop sia pausat le bras sobre un scalo de scala segon la latitut, e la ma sia extenduda a las partidas dejos, e l’autre cos sia suspendut de l’autre part, quar la junctura intra tantost.	 The physician places the patient's hands on a flat surface at an angle and extends his arm to prevent the internal hernia from falling out.
E cum le intrament de lu es complit segon quascuna maniera que es a tu possibla, e lahoras cove que tu pauses dejos le titillic spera de lana de engual quantitat; e aprop pauza emplastre perparat de polvera de moli am enses e album de huou sobre tot le muscle, ayssi quo es revolvut desus, e aprop strenh dejos le titillic am strictura decent; e le liament sia revolvut sobre le emplastre, e la ma de lu sia annectida al col de lu, e sia leyssat, e no sia mauguda la ma de lu per vii dias.	 With the help of a skilled attendant, the physician places them on the stretcher and spreads out their limbs as much as possible to prevent straining during transport or removal from muscle tissue damage.
E cove que sia pausada la vianda del malaute pauca, entro que·l membre sia confortat, quar es pus leugier a la sanacio de lu.	 The physician gently places the patient's member as little as possible, ensuring that their body is supported to facilitate healing and recovery.
E aprop la vianda sia donada major aprop vii o v e sia exercitat un movement; e donc si es fermat e no es mollificat, lahoras ja es sanat.	 The physician first gently places the patient's member but does not overly restrict it to prevent swelling or restriction of blood flow, and if fixed in position is maintained without relaxation after surgery, the physician has completed their work.
Mays si la junctura es dislocada motas veguadas per humiditat que accideys a lu o per autra causa, lahoras cove que en aquela sia administrat cauteri am tres traucs, segon que denant es dit en le capitol de cauteri.	 If the joint is dislocated due to humidity or other reasons, then doctors administer three incisions as mentioned in the chapter on surgery for its treatment.
E si tot aysso es fayt e aprop vii dias es desliat le liament e la junctura no es fermada, e le emplastre e la strictura son reduzitz sobre lu alcunas veguadas, e no es fermada e catz e no pot elevar aquel bras a las partidas desus, lahoras sapias que·ls nervis de lu, les quals so al cap del muscle, ja so inscizes o extendutz o mollificatz, e sapia que la junctura nul temps no sira ficada en loc sieu.	 When the ligament and joint are not fixed yet, and the space is reduced between the thighs, you have already opened this part to the patient's legs, placed a cushion under them, another on their chest, another on their hands holding them in place.
De la dislocacio de aquela qu’es fayta deves le pietz e la mamilha o las partidas detras, la reduccio es fayta am impulcio e extencio am las mas, entro que retorne.	 From the dislocation of that which you have already done on the back and buttocks, return to place the pillow or the mattress behind them, extending it as much as possible in front of where they are.
E sia administrada en aquela l’autra strictura, e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	 And having administered that other stretch, apply this one so that it heals completely
E si accideys aprop la sanacio gravitat en le membre e tarditat en le movement de lu, lahoras le malaute uze de banh motas veguadas entro que aquela gravitat sia alleujada e que retorne a la natura de lu primiera.	 And if the severe pain occurs in one of the legs and is accompanied by slow movements, doctors will apply gentle massages to relieve this gravity and return it to its normal state.
Capitol .xxvii.	 Chapter 27.
De curacio de dislocacio del coyde.	 Treatment of dislocation of the hip.
Sapias que la junctura del coyde es dislocada am difficultat e semblantment retorna am difficultat; e aquela es dislocada a totas partidas, e majorment a la partida denant a la partida detras, e la dislocacio de lu no es amaguada a tu quar es cazent dejos le vezement o dejos le tocament segon qualque figura sia dislocat, e quan ajustes le coyde disloguat am le sa, aquo es a tu declarat manifestament, quar la junctura es concavada e no pot doblar le bras, ni tocar am aquel le sieu muscle. E es que dos ministres extendan le bras, e tenguan aquel eyssament dos ministres per so que no sia remaugut deves la extencio.	 Two ministers are holding them apart to prevent the stretching from pulling their hands away too far.

After this procedure is completed, doctors should then tightly pull the joint back so it can be restored with a force.
