E aprop sia desliat; e donc si la junctura es formada en le sieu loc, lahoras tu deslia le liament de lu e layssa aquela.	 The next step is to loosen the joint and place a cushion over it, ensuring good support for the patient as they lie down.
E si vezas la junctura no be strenher, lahoras tu itera le emplastre e·l liament, e layssa aquela per alcus dias entro que sia extrenhuda; e aprop deslia aquela.	 If the joint is not stiff, apply some lubricant to help with mobility and place a cushion over it for support during treatment.
Mays si accideys a lu gravitat aprop la reduccio de la junctura, e la disposicio de lu es en movement, lahoras aministra humectacio en banh e fricacio subtil, e comprecio, entro que sia aleujat; o pausa sobre la junctura aleliati, so es coyssa de moto grassa; e aprop sia liada, e layssa aquela sobre le os le dia e la nueyt.	 If gravity becomes an issue when loosening the joint and movement occurs after that, apply a lubricant to lubricate it gently but not too much, compress tightly, keeping in mind that some looseness is necessary; pause over the joint occasionally as if you're trying to pull fat off of it, then place it on your elbow or knee.
E aprop osta aquela, e met aquel en banh; e quan suza, lahoras tu fregua la junctura am fricacio temprada, e aprop itera sobre aquela aleliati, so es ronhonal de moto, una veguada, e la segonda, e la .iii.a.,	 Once you've placed the cushion and applied lubricant as needed, ensure that any friction during loosening is minimized; when ready to treat, place it gently over the joint to support motion during treatment but not too hard for optimal movement.
am intrament de banh, entro que sia linit.	 The moment you're applying the lubricant, get ready as soon as possible.
E si voles, pausa sobre aquela fenda de vaca humida e scalfada am boder e stren sobre aquel; e fay aquo alcunas veguadas, quar aquela es humida e reduzeys a la sua disposicio.	 If you wish to, pause over the damp and cold area on your body while applying it to that joint; then apply some warmth after as needed to loosen it up further.
Capitol .xxviii.	 When pain occurs in the feet due to cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, it is commonly called gout by doctors
De curacio de dislocacio de malassen, so es de la junctura que es entre·l bras e la ma.	 During the dislocation of a joint, do not let your arm touch the other hand.
Malassen de la ma alcunas vetz es deslocada, e la reduccio de la dislocacio de lu es leugiera, e·l contrari es de las autras juncturas, mays empero cove que sia velocitat en la reduccio de lu en la hora en la qual es deslocada, denant que le loc sia apostemat o que accida en lu apostema caut.	 When dislocation occurs on one arm and the reduction of it happens gently, then contrary to other joints, however fast it should be done at the time of dislocation so that the location is not lost or if it were to occur in the location where the cautery was previously made.
E la reduccio de la dislocacio de lu es que tu pauses la junctura de la ma del malaute sobre una taula e le ministre extenda la ma de aquel, e le metge pause la sua ma o o la sua palma sobre la iminencia de la junctura, e empellisca aquela entro que retorne al sieu loc.	 The reduction of the dislocation is to place the patient's arm on a table and have the attendant extend the patient's hand towards it; then the doctor places their own hand or palm over the imminence of the joint, and pushes that back into its location.
Mays empero cove que sia considerat si la palma ja es ostada al ventre de la ma, lahoras le malaute pause le dos de la sua ma sobre una taula deves la extencio e la reduccio; e si la dislocacio es precedent deves le dos de la ma, lahoras sia la posicio de la ma de aquel intrinicequement sobre la taula, per so que la ma del metge caja sobre aquela iminencia de la junctura.	 If the patient's palm is already on their belly and there are no previous dislocations, then place both of the patient's hands on a table and have the attendant extend one; if the dislocation was previously done with one hand only, then position them intrinsically over the table so that the doctor's hand lies over the imminence of the joint.
E donc si retorna tantost, bon es; e sino, lahoras strenh aquela am empastre cedant le apostema e layssa aquel; e no iteres aquo, quar sino, no soferta ni no podes sobre la reduccio de lu pus que passan a lu dias.	 If that is the case then good, otherwise they will struggle with their arm pressed back and place it there; and if you do not agree or cannot, neither should be done nor can proceed to reduction without passing through them days.
Mays empero la junctura roman segon la sua tortuositat; e no notz al malaute alcuna causa, sino que la ma es mollificada e no pot strenher alcuna causa; lahoras sapias que les nervis son trincatz o trissatz, e lahoras no es engen en lu sino que sia strenhuda am cauteri prop le cazament de lu e fort leu aquo confereys alcuna causa.	 When joint pain is caused by a tortuous movement; and there is no cause for the patient other than its stiffness, softening it with gentle care can prevent any harm; knowing that nerves are strained or twisted because of this, doctors say that gout occurs due to excessive heat in the joints
Donc cum malassem es retornada, lahoras pausa sobre lu empastre le qual havem recomtat, e sia layssat e strenhut per v dias; e aprop sia desliat e sia layssat e la ma de lu sia excercitada.	 After the return of the intestine or hernia to its cavity is complete, gently massage it as recommended by doctors, and stretch it daily while also exercising the hand that held it tightly
Mays si le movement de lu es ostat e accideys en lu alcuna gravitat, lahoras leniys aquela am aygua cauda e am fricacio alcunas veguadas, entro que sia alleujat.	 If the movement of it is excessive and causes harm to its surrounding area or viscera, doctors will loosen that portion of the muscle as much as possible to alleviate any discomfort.
Capitol .xxix.	 The end
De la curacio de dislocacio dels ditz.	 From the care for dislocation of those things
Alcunas veguadas so dislocatz les ditz a tota partida.	 All the parts will be dislocated at once.
E quan es dislocat alcun dit de aquels al dos de la palma o al ventre de lu, lahoras sten le dit e impelleys la dislocacio de lu am les tieus pouses, entro que retorne.	 If any part of those things is dislocated between the two hands or in the stomach, then doctors will stretch it and try to prevent further dislocation by keeping both hands pressed together, until it returns to place.
E aprop sostenta le cap del dit, e suspen aquel deves la part a la qual es dislocat, e layssa aquel per dos dias.	 Then hold the head of the dislocated part and support that in the hand where it was dislocated with gentle care, stretching for two days.
E aprop suspen aquel e exten aquel entro que dreyt sia engualhat en aquel sieu dia.	 Then suspend it gently and stretch it continuously until both sides are even again.
E quan sira noyt, lia aquel segon aquela narracio, e no cesses desliar aquel en le dia e exercitar am movement, e lia aquel en la noyt; e fay aquo per alcus dias entro que sia streyt.	 When the second is done, I will then tell you another story and exercise that part of your body every day until it's finished; this may take several days to complete.
E fay semblant am aquo, si es dislocat al ventre de la ma, e lia aquel ad aquela partida e fay am aquo la tieua primiera operacio, entro que sia sanat.	 If the stomach is dislocated from the body's front, lie on that side and perform your first operation, making sure it heals properly.
E semblantment fay am aquo quan es dislocat a las autres partidas.	 Similarly, do this when you have dislocated any other parts of the body.
Capitol .xxx.	 [No meaning found]
De la curacio de dislocacio dels spondils del dos.	 The cure for dislocation of the spine from both sides.
Quan accideys ad alcun dels spondils del dos o del col dislocacio complida, e so remaugutz motz spondils de lors locs, lahoras en aquela no es curacio, quar la mort se coyta al malaute.	 If either of the two sides or the neck are dislocated and they cannot be restored to their normal position, then there is no cure; in fact death comes for the patient.
E senhal de aquo es que la egestio del malaute es fora-eyssida ses voluntat, e no pot retenir aquela; e motas veguadas so mollificatz alcus membres de lu o doas cambas de lu o dos brasses de lu, o un de aquels; o es remaugut un spondil de son loc, quar motas veguadas es remaugut e motas veguadas es fayta la remocio de aquels a quatre partidas.	 This means that the vomiting of the patient is outside their will and cannot be controlled; and any attempt to control it may make some of your muscles weak or do damage to your kidneys, liver, lungs, or any one of these organs; if you try to restore a spine back into its place, all attempts at restoration will fail, and all efforts made to restore the same will ultimately lead to death.
Donc aquela ja es remauguda a las partidas detras e es nompnada gelbozitat.	 So this has been done on both sides of it; no more attempt can be made after that
Mays la curacio de lu es que lahoras consideras si la gelbozitat accidey de puerissia, quar lahoras en aquela no es curacio ni de aquela no es sanacio de tot.	 The care of him is that the pain arises from cold humors infiltrating each part of the body, and pain occurs in the feet, it's customary for doctors to call this gout
Mays en aquela que ve per cazement o per percussio o per semblant ad aquels, ja diyssero les Antics las manieras de curacio am sermo prolixs, del qual lo mays retorna am profieyt; mays yeu ja e abreujat de aquel del qual lo pauc escusa del trop de lu, per la mieua propinquitat a la entencio mieua exposicio, am la qual he aquo expausat et format ex instrument divers de aquel am le qual mostrero aquo e espausero aquel.	 The care of him may also involve percussive or percussive percussion on such parts, the ancient ways of treatment being most effective in this case. The practitioner should have prepared instruments for this purpose and apply them to that part of his body, so as to remove the excess from it, by the close proximity to another part of the body mentioned previously
E dic que en gelbosita que accideys de la partida denant en le pietz, no es engen ni sanacio de aquela; e semblantment en aquela que es fayta a dos latz.	 The care may also involve treating the space between the patient's thighs and placing cushions under them, another servant on their legs, and another on their chest, holding their hands.
E de aquelas no es curada sino aquela que accideys en le dos propriament am aquo que yeu recomti.	 The care does not include treating the part of his body where it has already been mentioned above, but rather treatment on another part that is specifically recommended in this case.
E es que·l malaute sia extendut sobre la sua cara sobre pug engual prop de paret, e sia extendut dejos lu esturment molh per so que no sia lidit le pietz de lu.	 The patient should be laid flat on their back and have something wet applied to prevent the feet from being exposed.
E aprop un fust dreyt sia pausat, ficat en la terra en la extremitat del pug entorn le cap de lu, e autra fust en aviro les pes de lu en l’autra extremitat del pueg.	 Place a pillow flat on the ground near their head and also place one on each of their feet in the other extremity of their body.
E·l ministre tengua le fust, e no sia fermat en fossa; e autre ministre tengua l’autre segon aquela forma.	 When the minister has taken hold of it, let it not be fixed into a cavity; another minister takes the other one in that manner
E aprop envolopa sobre le cap del malaute e dejos les titillic liamen leon ferm; e exten la extremitat del liamel al fust le qual es deves le cap de lu, e lia aquel en lu; e aprop strenh l’autre liament sobre las ancas de lu les denols de lu, e deves las cambas de lu; e aprop ajusta totz les liamentz e lia aquels en l’autre fust le qual es deves les pes de lu.	 The first minister shall gently place it on the top of the patient and let them hold it firmly; another minister takes the other one in that manner, placing his arm around her hips to support her; and adjust all the straps so they are placed together on the opposite side from where he places the head of the mattress onto her.
E aprop le ministre cascu extenda le liament a la partida del fust, e no sian remaugutz les dos fustz e les liamentz dels sieus locs en les quals son ficatz, mays empero no so fermatz ayssi cum havem dit.	 The minister holding the straps should extend it to the foot of the mattress without removing the two feet and straps from their places where they are fixed; but not as firmly as we said before.
E le metge pause las suas palmas sobre le spondil am fortaleza entro que retorne, o que pause sobre aquela una taula, e aprop que ajuste sobre la taula les sieus pes entro que retorne.	 The doctor places their palms on the back of the neck and onto a table, and adjusts them so they are positioned at each end of the table when returning.
Mays si no retorna per aquesta forma, lahoras pren una taula de la qual la latitut o la longitut sia en aviro de tres brassas, e cava en la paret de la qual havem dit que es prop le malaute un loc en le qual intre la extremitat de la taula.	 If not returning by that method, the doctors place a table with its latitude or longitude set to three leagues, and face it in such a manner as described for the patient on one side of which they have already spoken.
E aprop pausa la maytat de la taula sobre le spondilh, e·l metge pause les sieus pes sobre l’autre extremitat, e estrenha be entro que le spondil sia coartat e que retorne al sieu loc.	 The doctor places their hands on the back of the neck and onto another side, ensuring that the head is properly positioned as they return to their location.
E si tu voles, obre am torn le qual es revolvut am la ma; e es que tu fiques en terra deves le cap del malaute en le derier del pug dos fustz, la longitut dels quals sia d’un bras, e deves le cap de lu en le derier del pug eyssament dos fustz; e sia la longitut que es entre quascun fust un palm, e ja es fayt en quascun fust trauc en le qual corr torn, e quascun sia mot fermat en terra per so que no sia maugut.	 "If you wish to lift up the leg that is bent upwards and place it on the ground in front of the other leg towards the foot side, make sure there are two fists' width between them; then take hold of its head with one hand and pull it towards your chest, ensuring there are still two fists' width between the fist you used to hold onto it and that part of the body.
E sia mes un fust redon en le qual es le torn, e sia revolvut en les dos traucs dels dos fustz.	 "After you have made a fist with one hand, bend both fists together towards each other in two steps.
E en la extremitat de lu es un trauc en le qual es format le fust, la longueza del qual es un palm am aquo que es revolvut; e en les dos autres fustz es semblant de aquel.	 "In the extremity of it there is a fist that has formed from it and its length matches the one you are using to bend; in both other fists they are similar.
E aprop strenh les liamentz que has streyt en le pietz del malaute en le trau le qual es deves le cap de lu, e les liamentz que has streyts en las coyssas de lu en le torn le qual es deves les pes de lu.	 "Secure the restraints that you placed on the patient's chest and arm to prevent them from pulling away when you are lifting up their leg.
E aprop deves quascun torn e stia un ministre que torssa le torn am la sua ma, e le metge engualhe le spondil segon que havem dit.	 "You should place one hand in the center of your chest and have another doctor hold onto it while you lift up the leg.
E aquesta es la forma del torn:	 "Here is how to perform the move:
E aprop pus que le spondil es retornat, e le loc es engualhat, lahoras cove que pauses empastre exciccatiu am album de huou, e aprop estopa; e aprop pause sobre le empastre astela de taula de la qual la latitut sia de tres ditz o enviro aquels, e la longitut de lu sia quantitat que prengua le loc de la gelbositat, e sobre la partida del spondil sa.	 "After the spinal cord is returned and its location has been established: pause briefly at a sharp edge of the table which length is three inches or longer; then place your hand over this area to stop it.
E aprop sia liat am liament le qual havem dit, e uze le malaute de nutriment subtil entro que sia sanat.	 When joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, it is customary to call gout for doctors.
E si roman alcuna iminencia en le loc en la fi de la sanacio, lahoras cove que sian aministradas medicinas que moilifico e liniscan am aministracio de la taula per lonc temps, la qual havem recomtada; e ja es aministrada en aquel loc lamina de plom.	 If there is no urgency in the location of the treatment or it should not be done immediately at the end of the healing process, then the remedies are to be administered gradually and for a long time according to what has been recommended; so that it can be applied at that location with a feather pad.
E alcunas veguadas accideys imminencia en le derier dels spondils del dos, e es cujat per aquela dislocacio; e es aquel os le qual ja imineys per que no cove que sia fayta prosompcio a lu am aquesta medicina, quar fort leu fara a tu accidir mort.	 Some of the reasons for urgency in the lower back are: the dislocation itself, and it is necessary to treat such an injury; then there may be those who have been advised not to apply this medicine due to its cold nature, which can cause frostbite if applied improperly, so do take care that you prevent such an accident.
Capitol .xxxi.	 31st chapter
De curacio de anca dislocada.	 The treatment of dislocated bones.
Sapias que la junctura del ancha e la junctura del muscle no endeve sino dislocacio tant solament, e no accideys ad aquelas aquo que accideys a las autras juncturas de petita remocio e concavitat.	 Joints of large and muscles cannot be dislocated only; but do not apply to those that happen in the other joints with small relief or indentation.
E la junctura de la ancha es dislocada segon quatre manieyras, quar es dislocada a las partidas dedintz, o a las partidas defora, o a las partidas denant, o a las partidas detras.	 The joint of the large is dislocated after four ways: it can be dislocated at the fingertips or on the forehand, inside, outside, front or back.
E majorment es dislocada a las partidas dedintz, e pauc a las partidas denant o a las partidas detras.	 However, it is most likely to dislocate in the direction of the fingertips and slightly towards the front or back.
E senhal de la dislocacio de lu a las partidas de dintz es quar, quan tu ajustas la camba del malaute sana am la malaute, es pus longua e·l denolh es pus heminent que de la sana, e·l malaute no pot doblar le sieu pe deves le lenguonar, e es le loc que siec le lengonar apostemat de apostema caut, per so que·l cap de la coyssa ja es pervengut aqui.	 When the joint is dislocated at a finger's tip or when you adjust the mattress of the patient and the patient becomes pain-free, then the leg must not be allowed to bend; it should remain stiff for fear that its head might protrude from between the cushions
E·l senhal de aquel al qual accideys dislocacio es a las partidas defora, es que les accidentz de lu so contraris ad aquest accident.	 The sentence refers to accidental dislocations being contrary to an intended dislocation (which is not specified in this context).
E senhal de aquel al qual accideys dislocacio a las partidas denant es quar expan la camba sieua segon compliment, mays empero no dobla aquela ses dolor que es en le denol, e si se perforsa ad anar e no pot sobre aquo a las partidas denant; e la urina de lu es retenguda e l’engonar de lu es apostemat, e deves la ambulacio de lu sobre le talo.	 If the dislocation occurs as mentioned and the mattress is stretched further than it can handle, then the pain that originates from this should not be bent or allowed to move around between the cushions; hold down the leg with both hands so its movement cannot cause harm.
E senhal de aquel al qual accideys dislocacio a las partidas detras es que no expande le denol, ni no puesca doblar aquel denant que doble le engonar, e la camba de lu es pus breva que l’autra, e l’engonar es mollificat, e·l cap de la coyssa es deves aquel loc.	 If the dislocation occurs behind and does not expand the pain or cause further movement of the leg that could bend it, then hold down the foot with both hands so its head cannot protrude between the cushions.
Mays reduccio de las specias de aquesta dislocacio es que tu consideras, lahoras, si la dislocacio es vetusta et antiqua, que ja es anticada am le havent aquela aprop tu aministras reduccio de lu e roman segon la sua disposicio, lahoras no es en aquela curacio de tot; e adonc no cove que en aquela sia fayta prosompcio.	 The goal of this procedure is to consider whether the dislocation has already healed and been cured by previous attempts at treatment if it is a persistent or recurring condition, in which case further treatment may not be necessary; otherwise you should proceed with reduction as usual.
Mays en aquel del qual la dislocacio es recent, e es una de las quatre specias de dislocacio, lahoras te coyta ad aquo que volvas la junctura e extendas aquela a las partidas dedintz e a las partidas defora, e mau aquela a la dextra e sinistra, quar fort leu retorna e no indigeys de autra cura.	 When the dislocation is recent and it's one of the four types of dislocations, then you should apply what follows to restore the joint and stretch it in both directions, ensuring that it returns gently without any other cure being needed
Mays, si no retorna en aquesta manieyra, lahoras cove que tu prepares ministre fort e extendas la camba de lu de la partida pus dejos, o am las suas mas, o am liament lo qual es liat sobre la camba desus le denol; e autre ministre extenda la ma de aquel desus enayssi que meta las suas mas dejos les titillics de lu; e aprop strenha am liament leon sobre la razit de la coyssa, e tengua autre ministre ters le extremitat del liament.	 If it does not return in this manner, then apply a strong stretch to the limb from which it occurred, stretching both sides of that limb separately, or across the chest if possible; and apply a hand strap on top of that limb so as to prevent any more hiccups from coming out.
E sia extencio de lu o de la partida dedintz a l’angonar a la partida de la furcula, o de la partida detras a la partida del dos.	 Stretch the arm towards the opposite arm or stretch across it if possible to prevent any more hiccups from coming out.
E sia la extencio de totz aquels en una veguada entro que·l malaute sia elevat am le sieu cos de terra e que romangua pendent.	 Stretch the whole body of that patient as much as possible towards the ground, and hold them in position while you wait.
E aquesta specia de extencio es specia cominal a totas quatre.	 This type of stretch is common to all four types.
E donc si la dislocacio retorna am aquo que havem dit, sira bo; e sino, lahoras es necessari a tota specia aquo que dire de la propria curacio.	 If the dislocation returns in the manner that we've described then yes, and if not, then you should apply another type of treatment based on your own judgement.
En la reduccio de lu propria, quan es dislocada, e la dislocacio es a las partidas dedintz, cove que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre le sieu latz sa; e aprop pausa les liamentz sobre la razit de la coyssa en aquel loc le qual entre le cap de la coyssa e·l loc que es dejos le langonar; e aprop exten le liament en sus de la part del angonar a la pus auta partida de la furcula.	 When the dislocation occurs at the base, when the dislocation is at the bottom of that arm, place your elbow on top of their head so as to prevent any more hiccups from coming out; and stretch across both elbows towards the top of the shoulder and the upper part of the arm next to it.
E aprop autre ministre fort prengua les brasses de lu, e amerme le loc gros de la coyssa malaute e extenda a las partidas deforo per extencio vehement, quar aquela retorna en le sieu loc.	 When you have placed the patient on their back and opened up space between their thighs with a cushion, prepare to insert a large cushion into the opening of the hernia, extend it towards the heart in order to force it out violently as soon as possible so that it returns where it belongs.
E aquesta specia es de pus leugiera curacio am la qual aquest membre es reduzit que las autres specias.	 This treatment is used when one member of the body has been reduced in size compared to others
Mays si es excusat sobre tu e no obezeys al entrament am aquesta specia de curacio de tot, lahoras cove que sian liatz les dos pes del malaute ensemps am liament fort, leugier, sobre amdos les talos e amdos les denols.	 When performing this treatment, hold both of the patient's legs tightly and firmly, supporting them at the bottom as well as their ankles.
E sia la longitut de quascun de son par la quantitat de quatre ditz, e sia la camba malaute extenduda mays que l’autre per quantitat de dos ditz.	 The length of each leg should be equal to the quantity of four spans, and the patient's bed should be extended more than the other by two spans.
E aprop le malaute sia suspendut sobre le cap del fust, e que sia en la mayso; e sia la longitut de lu de la terra la quantitat de dos brasses.	 Place the patient on their back facing upwards and make sure it is on a flat surface that measures two spans in length.
E aprop comanda a un jove fort que minuesca le cap de la coyssa, e sia suspendut am le malaute autre jove, e l’autre jove minuent la coysa am fortaleza empellesca, quar la junctura retorna al sieu loc am velocitat.	 Prepare a strong young man to reduce the size of the hernia and place him on top of the patient, with his knees at an angle that pushes it back into its proper location quickly.
Mays en la reducio propria, quan es dislocacio a la partida defora, cove que·l malaute jaga sobre pug segon que havem recomtat en le havent gelbozitat; e sia strenhut le liament sobre la camba malauta propriament e sobre le pietz de lu.	 When performing this treatment with the patient lying on their back and experiencing dislocation, you should ensure that they remain in place as tightly as possible while also holding them down by placing your hand firmly over their abdomen and chest.
E aprop dos fustz sian pausatz, la un als pes de lu, e l’autre al cap; e aprop sian pausatz fustz ajustatz al mieg del pueg ficat sobre·l qual draps humitz sian envolopatz, per so que·l malaute no sia dampnajat per que·l fust sia entre las coyssas de lu, per que deves la extencio a las partidas dejos no sia atirat.	 "Place the cushion under their buttocks and another on top of them; place one cushion beneath their head as well.
E aprop quascun ministre extenda a la sua part, e·l metge am la sua ma enguala la reduccio segon l’art.	 "The doctor extends his arm towards the patient and gently guides the reduction according to the art.
Donc, si obezeys a revercio, sira bo grandament; e sino, pausa sobre aquela diligentment e ayssi quo havem dit en gelbozitat per aquela engualment.	 "If the gout pain goes away by itself, it will be greatly relieved; if not, stop applying the pointed cautery and do as mentioned before.
Mays cove que·l malaute jagua sobre les sieus latz sa quetament.	 "The patient should lie flat on their back at once.
E quan la dislocacio es a las partidas denant, lahoras cove que la camba sia extenduda leugierament, e es segon aquesta meteyssa narracio sobre pueg; e le metge pause la palma de la sua ma dreyta sobre·l langonar malaute, e aprop coarte aquel am l’autra ma, e am aquela coartacio pausa aquel extendut a las partidas dejos a la partida del denol.	 "When the dislocation occurs on their lower limbs, they should gently stretch out their leg towards the doctor; and after that, tell the story of how to do it for them. The doctor places his hand over the patient's hand and guides the other arm to place a cushion under both legs at once.
E si la dislocacio es a las partidas detras, lahoras no cove que·l malaute sia extendut a las partidas dejos, e es elevat sobre la terra; habantz cove que sia pausat sobre causa dura, ayssi cum cove le eyssament si l’ancha de lu es dislocada a las partidas defora, segon aquo que havem dit del jasement de lu sobre dos anchas; e es sobre la sua cara e les liamentz sian extendutz, segon que havem dit, no ha guayre.	 "If the dislocation occurs on their upper limbs behind, they should not force them to stretch out both legs at once but instead lie flat on the ground; hold down their head and shoulders so that they cannot move, as mentioned before.
E cove que sia aministrada compressio am taula sobre le loc al qual yeys la junctura.	 The compression treatment should be applied to the location of the joint that experiences pain.
Donc cum la reducio es complida segon que cove — e·l senhal de la reduccio de lu no es amaguat a tu, e es que tu extendas del malaute doas cambas, e quan tu vezes aquelas enguals e le malaute extrenh la sieua camba e expandeys aquela ses excusacio, lahoras sapias que·l membre segon que cove es retornat — e lahoras tu ajusta doas coyssas e pausa empastre e extrenh am benda ayssi que la ancha no sia mauguda en alcuna de las partidas; e adheresca le malaute a repaus per tres dias o per quatre.	 After the reduction is complete and you extend both legs of the patient, when you pass over their groin area and expand that space, then the doctors know that the second member will be returned - and adjust two cushions and pause compression to stretch as wide so that it isn't too tight in any part.
E aprop deslia le liament e l’empastre, e compara la una camba am l’autra.	 After applying the reduction and compression, compare one leg with the other
Lahoras, si vezas aquelas enguals en vustament, lahoras sapias que la dislocacio ja es fermada, e adonc layssa le malaute anar.	 Then if you have stretched those fingers as wide as possible, the doctors know that the dislocation is fixed and you can remove the patient's foot now
E si vezas alcuna causa de mollificacio, lahoras tu retorna e emplastra aquel, e extrenh aquel segon la tua primiera strectura, e layssa aquel en tres dias.	 If there is no cause for mollification, the doctors return and stretch it again, extend that after your first stretch, then let that be stretched for three days.
E aprop deslia aquel, e fay aquel tardar en ambulacio sobre quascu per alcus dias, entro que sia confortat.	 After stretching that area, let it rest in mobility until you feel comfortable with it.
Capitol .xxxii.	 Chapter 22
De curacio de dislocacio del denolh.	 Treatment of dislocated fingers.
Le denolh es dislocat segon tres manieyras, quar es dislocat a las partidas defora, e a las partidas dedintz, e a las partidas dejos mays a las partidas detras; e a las partidas denant no es dislocat.	 The finger is dislocated after three attempts, if it is dislocated externally or internally and in between the joints; but if not dislocated at all then
E le senhal de dislocacio de lu es que comandes al malaute que aplique la sua camba am la coyssa; lahoras sapias que·l denol es dislocat.	 The first sentence seems to be a medical instruction for repositioning or realigning a hernia, specifically targeting the legs and chest areas of the patient. It commands the servant (possibly a physician's assistant) to apply a cushion on top of each thigh, as if it were a mattress, while holding the patient's hands in order to prevent any dislocation during this maneuver.
E la restauracio de totas las manieyras de lu es que fassas cezer le malaute dreyt, enayssi que ja extenda la sieua camba, si pot sobre aquo; adherir le tieu dos a la cara de lu, e pausa le pe de lu entre les tieus pes; e aprop fay adherir le denol de lu am las tuas palmas, e rete aquelas entre les tieus ditz sobre le denolh de lu am fortaleza, e autre ministre extenda le sieu pe entro que·l denol retorne a son loc.	 The second sentence is another medical instruction for repositioning or realigning the intestines back into place, this time targeting all of their parts (which I assume are organs). It commands the servant to first apply pressure on the patient's abdomen and thighs, then gently extend their belly, and finally hold both hands over the abdominal region while placing a cushion underneath them. The final instruction is to ensure that they return back into place once released from its restraining.
E senhal de reddicio de lu es que la sua camba adharesca am la coyssa am levitat no-laboroza.	 This sentence seems to be an additional instruction for the servant, possibly a physician's assistant or nurse, regarding the reinsertion of an organ back into its place in the patient's body. It commands the assistant to apply pressure on top of the patient's belly and thighs while lifting their legs off the ground, but without exhausting themselves (as indicated by "no-laboroza").
E aprop emplastra aquel e fay adhirir la camba am la coyssa, e aprop lia aquelas emsemps am una benda per tres dias o per quatre, e aprop deslia aquelas.	 This sentence seems to be another instruction for the servant, possibly a physician's assistant or nurse, regarding the application of pressure on top of the patient and their legs in order to reinsert an organ back into its place within the body. It commands the assistant to hold this cushion (possibly a mattress) onto the patient's belly while also securing it with a bandage for three or four days, and then removing it later.
E no uze le malaute de ambulacio per alcus dias, entro que sia sanat e cofortat.	 This sentence seems to be an instruction given to the patient regarding their mobility while they are recovering from surgery or injury. It commands them not to walk for a certain number of days so that they can heal and feel comfortable.
Mays si la reduccio de lu a tu es excusada, lahoras aministra fort extencio am liamentz dels quals en la curacio de la hancha precedit narracio.	 If the reduction to you is excused, the doctor will provide very strong and urgent remedies for any infection that may occur during treatment as a result of this narrative history.
Capitol .xxxiii.	 Chapter XXXIII
De la curacio de la dislocacio del talo.	 Of dislocation of the ankle
Le talo alcunas veguadas es remaugut per petita remocio, e alcunas veguadas es dislocat segon compliment, e la dislocacio de lu es fayta o a las partidas dedintz o a las partidas deforo.	 The ankle may be dislocated by stretching or the second blow, and dislocation of it is either called internal sprain or external sprain.
E le senhal de la dislocacio de lu es que vezes le talo imflat procedent a la partida a la qual es dislocat.	 It's important to note that the cause of dislocation could be flattening of the ankle at the time it is dislocated.
Mays la curacio de la remocio de lu es de leugiera reddicio, e es que sia extendut am facilitat am las mas e sia engualhat entro que retorne.	 The treatment for sprain may be to rest, and that both quick relief and healing time can vary greatly depending on severity.
Mays en la curacio de lu quan es dislocat segon compliment, cove que fasses cezer le malaute dreyt, e tengua aquel un ministre fort e valent de la partida detras del dos de aquel en le mieg loc de lu.	 When dislocation occurs as a result of the second blow, you should gently press on the area directly behind the two fingers that caused it and apply a very strong and urgent remedy for pain relief
E aprop te tu am la tieua ma dreyta le pe de la pus sobirana part, e am la tua ma sinistra de la part pus dejos del pe en le loc de la cavilha.	 Take your right hand to the top of your chest and place your left hand at the back of your head.
E aprop atira le pe a tu am la tua ma dreyta, e aprop am la sinistra per dos veguadas, e aprop exten am la sinistra; e empelleys le pietz del pe am la dreyta deves la camba ses trebalh.	 Take your right hand to the top of your chest and place both your hands on opposite sides, extend them in front of you, hold your head up with your left arm, and support yourself with your right arm for walking.
E fay aquo doas veguadas segon que havem comtat.	 When joint pain occurs due to cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, it customarily called gout by doctors.
E aprop empelleys le pietz del pe a la camba la tersa veguada, e tu es a la cavilha.	 And return the intestine or hernia back into its cavity and place your hand over that area to prevent it from coming out.
Donc si retorna en una veguada o en dos segon aquesta manieyra, e si vezes le pe engualhat, es bo; e sino, lahoras sobre lu itera la operacio, quar aquel retorna.	 Then if you return it in one or two attempts and the patient's foot stays intact, that is good; otherwise, doctors will perform surgery to remove it.
Mays si a tu es prohibida la reduccio de lu am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras fay jaser le malaute sobre le sieu dos sobre terra, e estrenh un paysel mot en terra fermat, e que caja entre las coyssas de lu, e tu ja has envolopat sobre lu drap per so que no ledesca le malaute.	 If the reduction of this hernia is forbidden and it was recommended by doctors, then place a cushion firmly on the ground under its two legs, put another cushion on the floor nearby, and keep your hand over that area to prevent the hernia from falling out.
E aprop le ministre de lu tengua las suas coyssas, e aprop autre ministre extenda le pe am las suas mas o am liament que lie sobre le col del pe; e aprop extenda aquel quascun ministre contre extencio del sieu par, e le payssel sia extant entre las coyssas del malaute retinent aquel, per so que·l cos de lu no sia atirat a las partidas dejos deves la sua extencio.	 The minister of that part should extend his leg over the patient's chest or abdomen and on to their side; another minister extends it against extending from its side towards the bottom of the leg, and keep a cushion between the thighs of the patient in place so that the patient does not lose his hold.
E aprop le metge enguala la dislocacio am las sieuas mas, e autre ministre tengua la coyssa sana a las partidas dejos, quar la dislocacio retorna am la facilitat.	 The doctor inserts into the healthy part of their leg and another minister holds on to the patient's thigh so that the dislocation returns in a comfortable position.
E donc cum retorna la dislocacio e es declarada a tu la sanetat de la reduccio de lu, lahoras pausa emplastre e extrenh aquela am liamentz fortment, e ligua le pe am liament a la camba.	 And once the dislocation is back in its place and declared to be healed from the reduction of it, doctors will continue holding their leg firmly as before, and make sure both legs are straight.
E cove que temes o te guardes dels nervis les quals so detras sobre le talo, per que le liament sobre aquel no sia vehement e leda aquel fortment.	 The first sentence of your text translates to "The nerves that run behind the tailbone must be protected from damage in order for it not to cause pain.
E aprop layssa aquel per dos dias o per tres; e si le liament es mollificat, extrenh aquel.	 You should support that part with two or three days, and if the discomfort is alleviated, hold on a little longer.
E aprop deslia aquel en le ters dia o en le quart, e prohibeys le malaute de anament per xl dias.	 Support it for one more day or four days, but do not let the patient strain themselves excessively in that time.
Mays si es forsat de anar denant aquel spazi, no es fayta segurtat que la dislocacio no sia sobre lu dissolvuda e corrumpuda, e aprop aquo que no recipia curacio.	 If you remove it right away, make sure the dislocation is not caused by damage to the bone or cartilage, and do what's necessary in order to correct any swelling that may arise.
E si accideys a lu apostema caut, lahoras cove que tu aministre en la cedacio de lu aquo en lo qual precedic la nostra narracio, en autre loc de curacio e de embrocacio, entro que sia remauguda.	 If the cautery is applied on that part where our narration previously mentioned it and another location for treatment and anointing, make sure all wounds are healed before proceeding with further care or anointing in order to ensure proper healing.
Capitol .xxxiiii.	 Chapter xxxiv
De curacio de dislocacio dels ditz dels pes.	 The treatment for dislocation of the feet.
Cove que aquel qu’es dislocat sia engualhat am pauca extencio ses trebal; e aquo que no es dificil, abantz es leugier.	 If it is dislocated gently support with minimal force and let go when done.
Mays si la dislocacio es en alcus nozes del dos del pe, lahoras cove que fassas cezer le malaute le sieu pe sobre loc engual de la terra o sobre taula, e sia estant ayssi cum si anava.	 If the dislocation is in both feet, make sure to lift the patient's head so that it rests on a flat surface or table, and hold them like you would if they were normal.
E aprop tu sta de pes, e pausa le tieu pe sobre aquo que imineys de las juncturas, e aprop calca aquel am le tieu pe am vertut entro que retorne, e que vejas aquel ja engualhat e no aparesca en le loc eminencia.	 Then support their feet and place their head on something like a pillow that is positioned against the joints, hold it in place as firmly as you would if they were normal, and keep them steady until you see them still and not appear anywhere else.
E aprop pausa dejos le ventre del pe de lu una taula que prengua tot le pe, a la qual sian dos caps, e aprop strenh aquel am strectura decent e ferma per tres dias; e aprop deslia aquel e fay aquel repausar de ambulacio per motz dias, entro que sia estrenhut e de reddicio sia assegurat.	 When you have opened the space between the patient's legs with a cushion placed under them and another servant on their legs, and another on their chest holding their hands, hold this first for three days; then remove it to allow free movement of the bowels for three days unless the bowel is completely healed or there is no discharge from it.
Capitol .xxxv.	 Chapter 55
De las specias de dislocacio que sian faytas am plagua o am fractura o am quascuna ensemps.	 Of the injuries that are caused by blows or fractures or any other kind of injury.
Quan accideys alcuna causa de aquelas, e tu te perforssas en la curacio de aquela e en la restauracio de lu, motas veguadas succezeys la mort.	 If the cause of these is not treated and you do nothing to heal or restore it, there will be a high risk that death will result.
E per aquo no cove que sobre la curacio de lu presuma, sino aquel que es savi en l’art, de lonc uzatge, misericordios e pietados, tardiu, no-ardit ni presomptuos; e que use en le comensament de medicinas que cedan apostemas cautz tant solament, e leyssa le malaute al divinal jutgament, sino ad aquel al qual speras salut de perdicio, am de la malautia alleviacio, e en la qual appareys alcuna speransa.	 It is not advisable to rely on the art of medicine alone, nor that which saves only by length of time and compassion; but rather it is better for one who uses medicines as a remedy from the outset with caution, so that good health may be obtained instead of or in addition to relief from disease.
E adonc esforsa te tantost far de lu la reduccio en le comensament de la causa, denant que endevengua apostema caut.	 Instead of using the remedy at an early stage when it is possible without risk
E adonc si le membre retorna segon que volem, lahoras aministra regiment le qual ceda apostema caut e cura la plagua am aquo que conveneys a lu dels enguentz desiccatius.	 Instead of administering the remedy to the member when it is possible without risk and curing the lesion at this point, it should be used as an ointment that has been prescribed with caution and cure the wound from the dry heat.
E si dislocacio es am fractura e accideys en le os satagias separadas, lahoras tu perforsa le stement de lor, e fay en aquo so que havem dit en las malautias simplas de aquo que es precedit en les locz de aquels.	 When a dislocation occurs and the separated bones are set to heal, the physician will perform this procedure in order for them to say that what was previously mentioned in those areas where it is preceded.
E guarda e esquiva segon la tua vertut aquel del intrament en las vias de temor segon que a tu es precedida la mia predicacio; quar aquo es milhor a tu deves le tieu Creator, e mays permanent a la tua gloria, e mays saludos al tieu cos verays aquels en le tieu temps.	 After this, guard and avoid the second one from the same way of fear as in previous times, for it is better to you by your own Creator, may be eternal with your glory, and many blessings to your body, true in these days.
Ayssi fineysso las paraulas de Albucasim perfieytament de las quals Dieus ne sia benezeyt.	 After saying the prayers of Al-Baqarah perfectly as he has mentioned it earlier
Amen.	 Ameen.
